<tr>
<th>Incipit
</th>
<td>&#160;
<ol><li> <img src="/images/lilypond/e15936e3d247b8b0f775c8710ba492db.png" alt=" \relative c' { \clef treble \compressFullBarRests R1*7^&quot;Allegro&quot; c2 r2 R1*4 r4 r8 g' d' g, d' f e4 r r2 r4 r8 g, d' g, d' f e4 } " />
</li><li> <img src="/images/lilypond/c5a77743db4145595f918218731b89c3.png" alt=" \relative c' { \clef treble \compressFullBarRests \time 6/8 \key f \major R8*6*8^&quot;Andante&quot; f8.( g16 a8) g( bes e,) f4( a8 c) r c~ c bes a~ a g f~ f e16( g f d c4) } " />
</li><li> <img src="/images/lilypond/1724b202a5c292c3d4c9069678699d7e.png" alt=" \relative g' { \clef treble \compressFullBarRests \time 2/4 R2*44^&quot;Allegro&quot; g4. c8 a4. c8 b d g, b c4 r8 c b d g, b c4 r8 c b16 c d b g a b g c4. } " />
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
